    var win = window;

      script.src = window.BOOMR.url;

      parent.appendChild(script);
    };
    if (!window.addEventListener && window.attachEvent && navigator.userAgent.match(/MSIE [67]./)) {

      bootstrap(parentNode, "boomr-async");

      win._boomrl = function() {
        bootstrap();
      };
